 saath hi jurmaana bharna pad saktaa he
 Let us tell you some important laws related to railways
 1
 It is a crime for women in a train to enter any male passenger in the reserve bogie
 agar koi mahila bogi main ghusata he, to us par jurmaana lag saktaa he
 Also TTE can remove such a male passenger from the bogey
 2
 Under Section 156 of the Railway Act, traveling on the roof, stairs, doors and engine of a train can lead to a jail term of three months
 saath hi jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he
 3
 railway act kii dhara 167 ke mutabik train main smoking karnaa jurm he
 Such people can be fined
 4
 If the TTE asks to show the ticket during the journey or after the end of the journey , the passenger must show the ticket
 aisa nahin karne par us yatri ke khilaaf karrwai kii ja sakati he
 5
 kisi ko sharaab pikar yaa nasha karke train main yatra karne or gaali-galouj karne kii ijaajat nahin he
 Along with taking such a person off the train, action can be taken against him under Section 145 of the Railway Act
 aise maamle main 6 maheene kii jail or jurmaane kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 6
 railway act kii dhara 141 ke tahat train main pheri lagaana yaa bheekh maangana bhi jurm he

 saath hi jurmaana bharna pad saktaa he
 7
 railway kii ijaajat ke bina kisi ko bhi train kaa tikat bechney kaa haq nahin he
 If someone is caught selling tickets, action can be taken against him under Section 142 of the Railway Act
 aise maamle main teen maheene kii jail or jurmaane kaa praavdhaan kiya gaya he
 8
 train main patharbaji karnaa sangeen aparaadh he
 In doing so, a provision of 10 years jail sentence and fine has been made under Section 150 of the Railway Act
 9
 Under Section 151 of the Railway Act, a person can be imprisoned for 5 years for arson or damage to the train
 saath jurmaana lagaaya ja saktaa he
 10
 railway act ke mutabik, agar koi vyakti sankraman beemaari se jujh rahaa he to usko train main yatra karne ke liye railway kii vishesh ijaajat leni hogi

 1

 4
